I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
$host() styles not synchronously available in onMount and $effect
### Describe the bug

Component styles are not synchronously available when using the $host() rune within onMount.

This prevents reliable access to computed styles, dimensions or CSS variables of the host element immediately after it's mounted.

This bug occurs in Svelte versions 5.36.0 through 5.36.13.
Svelte 5.35.7 it behaves as expected.

### Reproduction

1. Use svelte version 5.36.0 - 5.36.13.
2. Create a custom element
3. access $host() within onMount.

```svelte
<svelte:options customElement={{tag: "my-counter"}}/>

<script lang="ts">
  import {onMount} from "svelte";

  let Host = $host()

  $effect(() => {
    console.log("$effect", Host.shadowRoot?.innerHTML); // BUG: has no <style> tag
  })

  onMount(() => {
    console.log("onMount",Host.shadowRoot?.innerHTML); // BUG: has no <style> tag
    setTimeout(() => {
      console.log("delayed",Host.shadowRoot?.innerHTML); // has the <style> tag
    })
  })
</script>

<button class="btn">Counter</button>

<style >
  .btn {
    width: 123px;
    height: 123px;
  }
</style>
```

    94	                                }
    95	                                /** @param {string} name */
    96	                                function create_slot(name) {
    97	                                        /**
    98	                                         * @param {Element} anchor
    99	                                         */
   100	                                        return (anchor) => {
   101	                                                const slot = document.createElement('slot');
   102	                                                if (name !== 'default') slot.name = name;
   103	
   104	                                                append(anchor, slot);
   105	                                        };
   106	                                }
   107	                                /** @type {Record<string, any>} */
   108	                                const $$slots = {};
   109	                                const existing_slots = get_custom_elements_slots(this);
   110	                                for (const name of this.$$s) {
   111	                                        if (name in existing_slots) {
   112	                                                if (name === 'default' && !this.$$d.children) {
   113	                                                        this.$$d.children = create_slot(name);
   114	                                                        $$slots.default = true;
   115	                                                } else {
   116	                                                        $$slots[name] = create_slot(name);
   117	                                                }
   118	                                        }
   119	                                }
   120	                                for (const attribute of this.attributes) {
   121	                                        // this.$$data takes precedence over this.attributes
   122	                                        const name = this.$$g_p(attribute.name);
   123	                                        if (!(name in this.$$d)) {
   124	                                                this.$$d[name] = get_custom_element_value(name, attribute.value, this.$$p_d, 'toProp');
   125	                                        }
   126	                                }
   127	                                // Port over props that were set programmatically before ce was initialized
   128	                                for (const key in this.$$p_d) {
   129	                                        // @ts-expect-error
   130	                                        if (!(key in this.$$d) && this[key] !== undefined) {
   131	                                                // @ts-expect-error
   132	                                                this.$$d[key] = this[key]; // don't transform, these were set through JavaScript
   133	                                                // @ts-expect-error
   134	                                                delete this[key]; // remove the property that shadows the getter/setter
   135	                                        }
   136	                                }
   137	                                this.$$c = createClassComponent({
   138	                                        component: this.$$ctor,
   139	                                        target: this.shadowRoot || this,
   140	                                        props: {
   141	                                                ...this.$$d,
   142	                                                $$slots,
   143	                                                $$host: this
   144	                                        }
   145	                                });
   146	
   147	                                // Reflect component props as attributes
   148	                                this.$$me = effect_root(() => {
   149	                                        render_effect(() => {
   150	                                                this.$$r = true;
   151	                                                for (const key of object_keys(this.$$c)) {
   152	                                                        if (!this.$$p_d[key]?.reflect) continue;
   153	                                                        this.$$d[key] = this.$$c[key];
   154	                                                        const attribute_value = get_custom_element_value(
   155	                                                                key,
   156	                                                                this.$$d[key],
   157	                                                                this.$$p_d,
   158	                                                                'toAttribute'
   159	                                                        );
   160	                                                        if (attribute_value == null) {
   161	                                                                this.removeAttribute(this.$$p_d[key].attribute || key);
   162	                                                        } else {
   163	                                                                this.setAttribute(this.$$p_d[key].attribute || key, attribute_value);
   164	                                                        }
   165	                                                }
   166	                                                this.$$r = false;
   167	                                        });
   168	                                });
   169	
   170	                                for (const type in this.$$l) {
   171	                                        for (const listener of this.$$l[type]) {
   172	                                                const unsub = this.$$c.$on(type, listener);
   173	                                                this.$$l_u.set(listener, unsub);
   174	                                        }
   175	                                }
   176	                                this.$$l = {};
   177	                        }
   178	                }
   179	
   180	                // We don't need this when working within Svelte code, but for compatibility of people using this outside of Svelte
   181	                // and setting attributes through setAttribute etc, this is helpful
   182	
   183	                /**
   184	                 * @param {string} attr
   185	                 * @param {string} _oldValue
   186	                 * @param {string} newValue
   187	                 */
   188	                attributeChangedCallback(attr, _oldValue, newValue) {
   189	                        if (this.$$r) return;
   190	                        attr = this.$$g_p(attr);
   191	                        this.$$d[attr] = get_custom_element_value(attr, newValue, this.$$p_d, 'toProp');
   192	                        this.$$c?.$set({ [attr]: this.$$d[attr] });
   193	                }
   194	
   195	                disconnectedCallback() {
   196	                        this.$$cn = false;
   197	                        // In a microtask, because this could be a move within the DOM
   198	                        Promise.resolve().then(() => {
   199	                                if (!this.$$cn && this.$$c) {
   200	                                        this.$$c.$destroy();
   201	                                        this.$$me();
   202	                                        this.$$c = undefined;
   203	                                }
   204	                        });
   205	                }
   206	
   207	                /**
   208	                 * @param {string} attribute_name
   209	                 */
   210	                $$g_p(attribute_name) {
   211	                        return (
   212	                                object_keys(this.$$p_d).find(
   213	                                        (key) =>
   214	                                                this.$$p_d[key].attribute === attribute_name ||
   215	                                                (!this.$$p_d[key].attribute && key.toLowerCase() === attribute_name)
   216	                                ) || attribute_name
   217	                        );
   218	                }
   219	        };
   220	}
   221	
   222	/**
   223	 * @param {string} prop
   224	 * @param {any} value
   225	 * @param {Record<string, CustomElementPropDefinition>} props_definition
   226	 * @param {'toAttribute' | 'toProp'} [transform]
   227	 */
   228	function get_custom_element_value(prop, value, props_definition, transform) {
   229	        const type = props_definition[prop]?.type;
   230	        value = type === 'Boolean' && typeof value !== 'boolean' ? value != null : value;
   231	        if (!transform || !props_definition[prop]) {
   232	                return value;
   233	        } else if (transform === 'toAttribute') {
   234	                switch (type) {
   235	                        case 'Object':
   236	                        case 'Array':
   237	                                return value == null ? null : JSON.stringify(value);
   238	                        case 'Boolean':
   239	                                return value ? '' : null;
   240	                        case 'Number':
   241	                                return value == null ? null : value;
   242	                        default:
   243	                                return value;
   244	                }
   245	        } else {
   246	                switch (type) {
   247	                        case 'Object':
   248	                        case 'Array':
   249	                                return value && JSON.parse(value);
   250	                        case 'Boolean':
   251	                                return value; // conversion already handled above
   252	                        case 'Number':
   253	                                return value != null ? +value : value;
   254	                        default:
   255	                                return value;
   256	                }
   257	        }
   258	}
   259	
   260	/**
   261	 * @param {HTMLElement} element
   262	 */
   263	function get_custom_elements_slots(element) {
   264	        /** @type {Record<string, true>} */
   265	        const result = {};
   266	        element.childNodes.forEach((node) => {
   267	                result[/** @type {Element} node */ (node).slot || 'default'] = true;
   268	        });
   269	        return result;
   270	}
   271	
   272	/**
   273	 * @internal
   274	 *
   275	 * Turn a Svelte component into a custom element.
   276	 * @param {any} Component  A Svelte component function
   277	 * @param {Record<string, CustomElementPropDefinition>} props_definition  The props to observe
   278	 * @param {string[]} slots  The slots to create
   279	 * @param {string[]} exports  Explicitly exported values, other than props
   280	 * @param {boolean} use_shadow_dom  Whether to use shadow DOM
   281	 * @param {(ce: new () => HTMLElement) => new () => HTMLElement} [extend]
   282	 */
   283	export function create_custom_element(
   284	        Component,
   285	        props_definition,
   286	        slots,
   287	        exports,
   288	        use_shadow_dom,
   289	        extend
   290	) {
   291	        let Class = class extends SvelteElement {
   292	                constructor() {
   293	                        super(Component, slots, use_shadow_dom);
   294	                        this.$$p_d = props_definition;
   295	                }
   296	                static get observedAttributes() {
   297	                        return object_keys(props_definition).map((key) =>
   298	                                (props_definition[key].attribute || key).toLowerCase()
   299	                        );
   300	                }
   301	        };
   302	        object_keys(props_definition).forEach((prop) => {
   303	                define_property(Class.prototype, prop, {
   304	                        get() {
   305	                                return this.$$c && prop in this.$$c ? this.$$c[prop] : this.$$d[prop];
   306	                        },
   307	                        set(value) {
   308	                                value = get_custom_element_value(prop, value, props_definition);
   309	                                this.$$d[prop] = value;
   310	                                var component = this.$$c;
   311	
   312	                                if (component) {
   313	                                        // // If the instance has an accessor, use that instead
   314	                                        var setter = get_descriptor(component, prop)?.get;
   315	
   316	                                        if (setter) {
   317	                                                component[prop] = value;
   318	                                        } else {
   319	                                                component.$set({ [prop]: value });
   320	                                        }
   321	                                }
   322	                        }
   323	                });
   324	        });
   325	        exports.forEach((property) => {
   326	                define_property(Class.prototype, property, {
   327	                        get() {
   328	                                return this.$$c?.[property];
   329	                        }
   330	                });
   331	        });
   332	        if (extend) {
   333	                // @ts-expect-error - assigning here is fine
   334	                Class = extend(Class);
   335	        }
   336	        Component.element = /** @type {any} */ Class;
   337	        return Class;
   338	}
   339

     5	/**
     6	 * @param {Node} anchor
     7	 * @param {{ hash: string, code: string }} css
     8	 */
     9	export function append_styles(anchor, css) {
    10	        // Use `queue_micro_task` to ensure `anchor` is in the DOM, otherwise getRootNode() will yield wrong results
    11	        queue_micro_task(() => {
    12	                var root = anchor.getRootNode();
    13	
    14	                var target = /** @type {ShadowRoot} */ (root).host
    15	                        ? /** @type {ShadowRoot} */ (root)
    16	                        : /** @type {Document} */ (root).head ?? /** @type {Document} */ (root.ownerDocument).head;
    17	
    18	                // Always querying the DOM is roughly the same perf as additionally checking for presence in a map first assuming
    19	                // that you'll get cache hits half of the time, so we just always query the dom for simplicity and code savings.
    20	                if (!target.querySelector('#' + css.hash)) {
    21	                        const style = document.createElement('style');
    22	                        style.id = css.hash;
    23	                        style.textContent = css.code;
    24	
    25	                        target.appendChild(style);
    26	
    27	                        if (DEV) {
    28	                                register_style(css.hash, style);
    29	                        }
    30	                }
    31	        });
    32	}

    35	/**
    36	 * This is normally true — block effects should run their intro transitions —
    37	 * but is false during hydration (unless `options.intro` is `true`) and
    38	 * when creating the children of a `<svelte:element>` that just changed tag

    40	export let should_intro = true;

    47	/**
    48	 * @param {Element} text
    49	 * @param {string} value
    50	 * @returns {void}
    51	 */
    52	export function set_text(text, value) {
    53	        // For objects, we apply string coercion (which might make things like $state array references in the template reactive) before diffing
    54	        var str = value == null ? '' : typeof value === 'object' ? value + '' : value;
    55	        // @ts-expect-error
    56	        if (str !== (text.__t ??= text.nodeValue)) {
    57	                // @ts-expect-error
    58	                text.__t = str;
    59	                text.nodeValue = str + '';
    60	        }
    61	}
    62	
    63	/**
    64	 * Mounts a component to the given target and returns the exports and potentially the props (if compiled with `accessors: true`) of the component.
    65	 * Transitions will play during the initial render unless the `intro` option is set to `false`.
    66	 *
    67	 * @template {Record<string, any>} Props
    68	 * @template {Record<string, any>} Exports
    69	 * @param {ComponentType<SvelteComponent<Props>> | Component<Props, Exports, any>} component
    70	 * @param {MountOptions<Props>} options
    71	 * @returns {Exports}
    72	 */
    73	export function mount(component, options) {
    74	        return _mount(component, options);
    75	}
    76	
    77	/**
    78	 * Hydrates a component on the given target and returns the exports and potentially the props (if compiled with `accessors: true`) of the component
    79	 *
    80	 * @template {Record<string, any>} Props
    81	 * @template {Record<string, any>} Exports
    82	 * @param {ComponentType<SvelteComponent<Props>> | Component<Props, Exports, any>} component
    83	 * @param {{} extends Props ? {
    84	 *              target: Document | Element | ShadowRoot;
    85	 *              props?: Props;
    86	 *              events?: Record<string, (e: any) => any>;
    87	 *      context?: Map<any, any>;
    88	 *              intro?: boolean;
    89	 *              recover?: boolean;
    90	 *      } : {
    91	 *              target: Document | Element | ShadowRoot;
    92	 *              props: Props;
    93	 *              events?: Record<string, (e: any) => any>;
    94	 *      context?: Map<any, any>;
    95	 *              intro?: boolean;
    96	 *              recover?: boolean;
    97	 *      }} options
    98	 * @returns {Exports}
    99	 */
   100	export function hydrate(component, options) {
   101	        init_operations();
   102	        options.intro = options.intro ?? false;
   103	        const target = options.target;
   104	        const was_hydrating = hydrating;
   105	        const previous_hydrate_node = hydrate_node;
   106	
   107	        try {
   108	                var anchor = /** @type {TemplateNode} */ (get_first_child(target));
   109	                while (
   110	                        anchor &&
   111	                        (anchor.nodeType !== COMMENT_NODE || /** @type {Comment} */ (anchor).data !== HYDRATION_START)
   112	                ) {
   113	                        anchor = /** @type {TemplateNode} */ (get_next_sibling(anchor));
   114	                }
   115	
   116	                if (!anchor) {
   117	                        throw HYDRATION_ERROR;
   118	                }
   119	
   120	                set_hydrating(true);
   121	                set_hydrate_node(/** @type {Comment} */ (anchor));
   122	                hydrate_next();
   123	
   124	                const instance = _mount(component, { ...options, anchor });
   125	
   126	                if (
   127	                        hydrate_node === null ||
   128	                        hydrate_node.nodeType !== COMMENT_NODE ||
   129	                        /** @type {Comment} */ (hydrate_node).data !== HYDRATION_END
   130	                ) {
   131	                        w.hydration_mismatch();
   132	                        throw HYDRATION_ERROR;
   133	                }
   134	
   135	                set_hydrating(false);
   136	
   137	                return /**  @type {Exports} */ (instance);
   138	        } catch (error) {
   139	                if (error === HYDRATION_ERROR) {
   140	                        if (options.recover === false) {
   141	                                e.hydration_failed();
   142	                        }
   143	
   144	                        // If an error occured above, the operations might not yet have been initialised.
   145	                        init_operations();
   146	                        clear_text_content(target);
   147	
   148	                        set_hydrating(false);
   149	                        return mount(component, options);
   150	                }
   151	
   152	                throw error;
   153	        } finally {
   154	                set_hydrating(was_hydrating);
   155	                set_hydrate_node(previous_hydrate_node);
   156	                reset_head_anchor();
   157	        }
   158	}
   159	
   160	/** @type {Map<string, number>} */
   161	const document_listeners = new Map();
   162	
   163	/**
   164	 * @template {Record<string, any>} Exports
   165	 * @param {ComponentType<SvelteComponent<any>> | Component<any>} Component
   166	 * @param {MountOptions} options
   167	 * @returns {Exports}
   168	 */
   169	function _mount(Component, { target, anchor, props = {}, events, context, intro = true }) {
   170	        init_operations();
   171	
   172	        var registered_events = new Set();
   173	
   174	        /** @param {Array<string>} events */
   175	        var event_handle = (events) => {
   176	                for (var i = 0; i < events.length; i++) {
   177	                        var event_name = events[i];
   178	
   179	                        if (registered_events.has(event_name)) continue;
   180	                        registered_events.add(event_name);
   181	
   182	                        var passive = is_passive_event(event_name);
   183	
   184	                        // Add the event listener to both the container and the document.
   185	                        // The container listener ensures we catch events from within in case
   186	                        // the outer content stops propagation of the event.
   187	                        target.addEventListener(event_name, handle_event_propagation, { passive });
   188	
   189	                        var n = document_listeners.get(event_name);
   190	
   191	                        if (n === undefined) {
   192	                                // The document listener ensures we catch events that originate from elements that were
   193	                                // manually moved outside of the container (e.g. via manual portals).
   194	                                document.addEventListener(event_name, handle_event_propagation, { passive });
   195	                                document_listeners.set(event_name, 1);
   196	                        } else {
   197	                                document_listeners.set(event_name, n + 1);
   198	                        }
   199	                }
   200	        };
   201	
   202	        event_handle(array_from(all_registered_events));
   203	        root_event_handles.add(event_handle);
   204	
   205	        /** @type {Exports} */
   206	        // @ts-expect-error will be defined because the render effect runs synchronously
   207	        var component = undefined;
   208	
   209	        var unmount = component_root(() => {
   210	                var anchor_node = anchor ?? target.appendChild(create_text());
   211	
   212	                branch(() => {
   213	                        if (context) {
   214	                                push({});
   215	                                var ctx = /** @type {ComponentContext} */ (component_context);
   216	                                ctx.c = context;
   217	                        }
   218	
   219	                        if (events) {
   220	                                // We can't spread the object or else we'd lose the state proxy stuff, if it is one
   221	                                /** @type {any} */ (props).$$events = events;
   222	                        }
   223	
   224	                        if (hydrating) {
   225	                                assign_nodes(/** @type {TemplateNode} */ (anchor_node), null);
   226	                        }
   227	
   228	                        should_intro = intro;
   229	                        // @ts-expect-error the public typings are not what the actual function looks like
   230	                        component = Component(anchor_node, props) || {};
   231	                        should_intro = true;
   232	
   233	                        if (hydrating) {
   234	                                /** @type {Effect} */ (active_effect).nodes_end = hydrate_node;
   235	                        }
   236	
   237	                        if (context) {
   238	                                pop();
   239	                        }
   240	                });
   241	
   242	                return () => {
   243	                        for (var event_name of registered_events) {
   244	                                target.removeEventListener(event_name, handle_event_propagation);
   245	
   246	                                var n = /** @type {number} */ (document_listeners.get(event_name));
   247	
   248	                                if (--n === 0) {
   249	                                        document.removeEventListener(event_name, handle_event_propagation);
   250	                                        document_listeners.delete(event_name);
   251	                                } else {
   252	                                        document_listeners.set(event_name, n);
   253	                                }
   254	                        }
   255	
   256	                        root_event_handles.delete(event_handle);
   257	
   258	                        if (anchor_node !== anchor) {
   259	                                anchor_node.parentNode?.removeChild(anchor_node);
   260	                        }
   261	                };
   262	        });
   263	
   264	        mounted_components.set(component, unmount);
   265	        return component;
   266	}
   267	
   268	/**
   269	 * References of the components that were mounted or hydrated.
   270	 * Uses a `WeakMap` to avoid memory leaks.
   271	 */
   272	let mounted_components = new WeakMap();
   273	
   274	/**
   275	 * Unmounts a component that was previously mounted using `mount` or `hydrate`.
   276	 *
   277	 * Since 5.13.0, if `options.outro` is `true`, [transitions](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/transition) will play before the component is removed from the DOM.
   278	 *
   279	 * Returns a `Promise` that resolves after transitions have completed if `options.outro` is true, or immediately otherwise (prior to 5.13.0, returns `void`).
   280	 *
   281	 * ```js
   282	 * import { mount, unmount } from 'svelte';
   283	 * import App from './App.svelte';
   284	 *
   285	 * const app = mount(App, { target: document.body });
   286	 *
   287	 * // later...
   288	 * unmount(app, { outro: true });
   289	 * ```
   290	 * @param {Record<string, any>} component
   291	 * @param {{ outro?: boolean }} [options]
   292	 * @returns {Promise<void>}
   293	 */
   294	export function unmount(component, options) {
   295	        const fn = mounted_components.get(component);
   296	
   297	        if (fn) {
   298	                mounted_components.delete(component);
   299	                return fn(options);
   300	        }
   301	
   302	        if (DEV) {
   303	                w.lifecycle_double_unmount();
   304	        }
   305	
   306	        return Promise.resolve();
   307	}

     3	// Fallback for when requestIdleCallback is not available
     4	const request_idle_callback =
     5	        typeof requestIdleCallback === 'undefined'
     6	                ? (/** @type {() => void} */ cb) => setTimeout(cb, 1)
     7	                : requestIdleCallback;

     9	/** @type {Array<() => void>} */
    10	let micro_tasks = [];
    11	
    12	/** @type {Array<() => void>} */
    13	let idle_tasks = [];
    14	
    15	function run_micro_tasks() {
    16	        var tasks = micro_tasks;
    17	        micro_tasks = [];
    18	        run_all(tasks);
    19	}
    20	
    21	function run_idle_tasks() {
    22	        var tasks = idle_tasks;
    23	        idle_tasks = [];
    24	        run_all(tasks);
    25	}
    26	
    27	/**
    28	 * @param {() => void} fn
    29	 */
    30	export function queue_micro_task(fn) {
    31	        if (micro_tasks.length === 0) {
    32	                queueMicrotask(run_micro_tasks);
    33	        }
    34	
    35	        micro_tasks.push(fn);
    36	}

    38	/**
    39	 * @param {() => void} fn
    40	 */
    41	export function queue_idle_task(fn) {
    42	        if (idle_tasks.length === 0) {
    43	                request_idle_callback(run_idle_tasks);
    44	        }
    45	
    46	        idle_tasks.push(fn);
    47	}

    76	let last_scheduled_effect = null;
    77	
    78	let is_flushing = false;
    79	
    80	let is_flushing_sync = false;
    81	export class Batch {
    82	        /**
    83	         * The current values of any sources that are updated in this batch
    84	         * They keys of this map are identical to `this.#previous`
    85	         * @type {Map<Source, any>}
    86	         */
    87	        current = new Map();
    88	
    89	        /**
    90	         * The values of any sources that are updated in this batch _before_ those updates took place.
    91	         * They keys of this map are identical to `this.#current`
    92	         * @type {Map<Source, any>}
    93	         */
    94	        #previous = new Map();
    95	
    96	        /**
    97	         * When the batch is committed (and the DOM is updated), we need to remove old branches
    98	         * and append new ones by calling the functions added inside (if/each/key/etc) blocks
    99	         * @type {Set<() => void>}
   100	         */
   101	        #callbacks = new Set();
   102	
   103	        /**
   104	         * The number of async effects that are currently in flight
   105	         */
   106	        #pending = 0;
   107	
   108	        /**
   109	         * A deferred that resolves when the batch is committed, used with `settled()`
   110	         * TODO replace with Promise.withResolvers once supported widely enough
   111	         * @type {{ promise: Promise<void>, resolve: (value?: any) => void, reject: (reason: unknown) => void } | null}
   112	         */
   113	        #deferred = null;
   114	
   115	        /**
   116	         * True if an async effect inside this batch resolved and
   117	         * its parent branch was already deleted
   118	         */
   119	        #neutered = false;
   120	
   121	        /**
   122	         * Async effects (created inside `async_derived`) encountered during processing.
   123	         * These run after the rest of the batch has updated, since they should
   124	         * always have the latest values
   125	         * @type {Effect[]}
   126	         */
   127	        #async_effects = [];
   128	
   129	        /**
   130	         * The same as `#async_effects`, but for effects inside a newly-created
   131	         * `<svelte:boundary>` — these do not prevent the batch from committing
   132	         * @type {Effect[]}
   133	         */
   134	        #boundary_async_effects = [];
   135	
   136	        /**
   137	         * Template effects and `$effect.pre` effects, which run when
   138	         * a batch is committed
   139	         * @type {Effect[]}
   140	         */
   141	        #render_effects = [];
   142	
   143	        /**
   144	         * The same as `#render_effects`, but for `$effect` (which runs after)
   145	         * @type {Effect[]}
   146	         */
   147	        #effects = [];
   148	
   149	        /**
   150	         * Block effects, which may need to re-run on subsequent flushes
   151	         * in order to update internal sources (e.g. each block items)
   152	         * @type {Effect[]}
   153	         */
   154	        #block_effects = [];
   155	
   156	        /**
   157	         * Deferred effects (which run after async work has completed) that are DIRTY
   158	         * @type {Effect[]}
   159	         */
   160	        #dirty_effects = [];
   161	
   162	        /**
   163	         * Deferred effects that are MAYBE_DIRTY
   164	         * @type {Effect[]}
   165	         */
   166	        #maybe_dirty_effects = [];
   167	
   168	        /**
   169	         * A set of branches that still exist, but will be destroyed when this batch
   170	         * is committed — we skip over these during `process`
   171	         * @type {Set<Effect>}
   172	         */
   173	        skipped_effects = new Set();
   174	
   175	        /**
   176	         *
   177	         * @param {Effect[]} root_effects
   178	         */
   179	        process(root_effects) {
   180	                queued_root_effects = [];
   181	
   182	                previous_batch = null;
   183	
   184	                /** @type {Map<Source, { v: unknown, wv: number }> | null} */
   185	                var current_values = null;
   186	
   187	                // if there are multiple batches, we are 'time travelling' —
   188	                // we need to undo the changes belonging to any batch
   189	                // other than the current one
   190	                if (batches.size > 1) {
   191	                        current_values = new Map();
   192	                        batch_deriveds = new Map();
   193	
   194	                        for (const [source, current] of this.current) {
   195	                                current_values.set(source, { v: source.v, wv: source.wv });
   196	                                source.v = current;
   197	                        }
   198	
   199	                        for (const batch of batches) {
   200	                                if (batch === this) continue;
   201	
   202	                                for (const [source, previous] of batch.#previous) {
   203	                                        if (!current_values.has(source)) {
   204	                                                current_values.set(source, { v: source.v, wv: source.wv });
   205	                                                source.v = previous;
   206	                                        }
   207	                                }
   208	                        }
   209	                }
   210	
   211	                for (const root of root_effects) {
   212	                        this.#traverse_effect_tree(root);
   213	                }
   214	
   215	                // if we didn't start any new async work, and no async work
   216	                // is outstanding from a previous flush, commit
   217	                if (this.#async_effects.length === 0 && this.#pending === 0) {
   218	                        this.#commit();
   219	
   220	                        var render_effects = this.#render_effects;
   221	                        var effects = this.#effects;
   222	
   223	                        this.#render_effects = [];
   224	                        this.#effects = [];
   225	                        this.#block_effects = [];
   226	
   227	                        // If sources are written to, then work needs to happen in a separate batch, else prior sources would be mixed with
   228	                        // newly updated sources, which could lead to infinite loops when effects run over and over again.
   229	                        previous_batch = current_batch;
   230	                        current_batch = null;
   231	
   232	                        flush_queued_effects(render_effects);
   233	                        flush_queued_effects(effects);
   234	
   235	                        // Reinstate the current batch if there was no new one created, as `process()` runs in a loop in `flush_effects()`.
   236	                        // That method expects `current_batch` to be set, and could run the loop again if effects result in new effects
   237	                        // being scheduled but without writes happening in which case no new batch is created.
   238	                        if (current_batch === null) {
   239	                                current_batch = this;
   240	                        } else {
   241	                                batches.delete(this);
   242	                        }
   243	
   244	                        this.#deferred?.resolve();
   245	                } else {
   246	                        this.#defer_effects(this.#render_effects);
   247	                        this.#defer_effects(this.#effects);
   248	                        this.#defer_effects(this.#block_effects);
   249	                }
   250	
   251	                if (current_values) {
   252	                        for (const [source, { v, wv }] of current_values) {
   253	                                // reset the source to the current value (unless
   254	                                // it got a newer value as a result of effects running)
   255	                                if (source.wv <= wv) {
   256	                                        source.v = v;
   257	                                }
   258	                        }
   259	
   260	                        batch_deriveds = null;
   261	                }
   262	
   263	                for (const effect of this.#async_effects) {
   264	                        update_effect(effect);
   265	                }
   266	
   267	                for (const effect of this.#boundary_async_effects) {
   268	                        update_effect(effect);
   269	                }
   270	
   271	                this.#async_effects = [];
   272	                this.#boundary_async_effects = [];
   273	        }
   274	
   275	        /**
   276	         * Traverse the effect tree, executing effects or stashing
   277	         * them for later execution as appropriate
   278	         * @param {Effect} root
   279	         */
   280	        #traverse_effect_tree(root) {
   281	                root.f ^= CLEAN;
   282	
   283	                var effect = root.first;
   284	
   285	                while (effect !== null) {
   286	                        var flags = effect.f;
   287	                        var is_branch = (flags & (BRANCH_EFFECT | ROOT_EFFECT)) !== 0;
   288	                        var is_skippable_branch = is_branch && (flags & CLEAN) !== 0;
   289	
   290	                        var skip = is_skippable_branch || (flags & INERT) !== 0 || this.skipped_effects.has(effect);
   291	
   292	                        if (!skip && effect.fn !== null) {
   293	                                if (is_branch) {
   294	                                        effect.f ^= CLEAN;
   295	                                } else if ((flags & CLEAN) === 0) {
   296	                                        if ((flags & EFFECT) !== 0) {
   297	                                                this.#effects.push(effect);
   298	                                        } else if (async_mode_flag && (flags & RENDER_EFFECT) !== 0) {
   299	                                                this.#render_effects.push(effect);
   300	                                        } else if ((flags & ASYNC) !== 0) {
   301	                                                var effects = effect.b?.pending ? this.#boundary_async_effects : this.#async_effects;
   302	                                                effects.push(effect);
   303	                                        } else if (is_dirty(effect)) {
   304	                                                if ((effect.f & BLOCK_EFFECT) !== 0) this.#block_effects.push(effect);
   305	                                                update_effect(effect);
   306	                                        }
   307	                                }
   308	
   309	                                var child = effect.first;
   310	
   311	                                if (child !== null) {
   312	                                        effect = child;
   313	                                        continue;
   314	                                }
   315	                        }
   316	
   317	                        var parent = effect.parent;
   318	                        effect = effect.next;
   319	
   320	                        while (effect === null && parent !== null) {
   321	                                effect = parent.next;
   322	                                parent = parent.parent;
   323	                        }
   324	                }
   325	        }
   326	
   327	        /**
   328	         * @param {Effect[]} effects
   329	         */
   330	        #defer_effects(effects) {
   331	                for (const e of effects) {
   332	                        const target = (e.f & DIRTY) !== 0 ? this.#dirty_effects : this.#maybe_dirty_effects;
   333	                        target.push(e);
   334	
   335	                        // mark as clean so they get scheduled if they depend on pending async state
   336	                        set_signal_status(e, CLEAN);
   337	                }
   338	
   339	                effects.length = 0;
   340	        }
   341	
   342	        /**
   343	         * Associate a change to a given source with the current
   344	         * batch, noting its previous and current values
   345	         * @param {Source} source
   346	         * @param {any} value
   347	         */
   348	        capture(source, value) {
   349	                if (!this.#previous.has(source)) {
   350	                        this.#previous.set(source, value);
   351	                }
   352	
   353	                this.current.set(source, source.v);
   354	        }
   355	
   356	        activate() {
   357	                current_batch = this;
   358	        }
   359	
   360	        deactivate() {
   361	                current_batch = null;
   362	                previous_batch = null;
   363	
   364	                for (const update of effect_pending_updates) {
   365	                        effect_pending_updates.delete(update);
   366	                        update();
   367	
   368	                        if (current_batch !== null) {
   369	                                // only do one at a time
   370	                                break;
   371	                        }
   372	                }
   373	        }
   374	
   375	        neuter() {
   376	                this.#neutered = true;
   377	        }
   378	
   379	        flush() {
   380	                if (queued_root_effects.length > 0) {
   381	                        flush_effects();
   382	                } else {
   383	                        this.#commit();
   384	                }
   385	
   386	                if (current_batch !== this) {
   387	                        // this can happen if a `flushSync` occurred during `flush_effects()`,
   388	                        // which is permitted in legacy mode despite being a terrible idea
   389	                        return;
   390	                }
   391	
   392	                if (this.#pending === 0) {
   393	                        batches.delete(this);
   394	                }
   395	
   396	                this.deactivate();
   397	        }
   398	
   399	        /**
   400	         * Append and remove branches to/from the DOM
   401	         */
   402	        #commit() {
   403	                if (!this.#neutered) {
   404	                        for (const fn of this.#callbacks) {
   405	                                fn();
   406	                        }
   407	                }
   408	
   409	                this.#callbacks.clear();
   410	        }
   411	
   412	        increment() {
   413	                this.#pending += 1;
   414	        }
   415	
   416	        decrement() {
   417	                this.#pending -= 1;
   418	
   419	                if (this.#pending === 0) {
   420	                        for (const e of this.#dirty_effects) {
   421	                                set_signal_status(e, DIRTY);
   422	                                schedule_effect(e);
   423	                        }
   424	
   425	                        for (const e of this.#maybe_dirty_effects) {
   426	                                set_signal_status(e, MAYBE_DIRTY);
   427	                                schedule_effect(e);
   428	                        }
   429	
   430	                        this.#render_effects = [];
   431	                        this.#effects = [];
   432	
   433	                        this.flush();
   434	                } else {
   435	                        this.deactivate();
   436	                }
   437	        }
   438	
   439	        /** @param {() => void} fn */
   440	        add_callback(fn) {
   441	                this.#callbacks.add(fn);
   442	        }
   443	
   444	        settled() {
   445	                return (this.#deferred ??= deferred()).promise;
   446	        }
   447	
   448	        static ensure() {
   449	                if (current_batch === null) {
   450	                        const batch = (current_batch = new Batch());
   451	                        batches.add(current_batch);
   452	
   453	                        if (!is_flushing_sync) {
   454	                                Batch.enqueue(() => {
   455	                                        if (current_batch !== batch) {
   456	                                                // a flushSync happened in the meantime
   457	                                                return;
   458	                                        }
   459	
   460	                                        batch.flush();
   461	                                });
   462	                        }
   463	                }
   464	
   465	                return current_batch;
   466	        }
   467	
   468	        /** @param {() => void} task */
   469	        static enqueue(task) {
   470	                if (tasks.length === 0) {
   471	                        queueMicrotask(dequeue);
   472	                }
   473	
   474	                tasks.unshift(task);
   475	        }
   476	}
   477	
   478	/**
   479	 * Synchronously flush any pending updates.
   480	 * Returns void if no callback is provided, otherwise returns the result of calling the callback.
   481	 * @template [T=void]
   482	 * @param {(() => T) | undefined} [fn]
   483	 * @returns {T}
   484	 */
   485	export function flushSync(fn) {
   486	        if (async_mode_flag && active_effect !== null) {
   487	                e.flush_sync_in_effect();
   488	        }
   489	
   490	        var was_flushing_sync = is_flushing_sync;
   491	        is_flushing_sync = true;
   492	
   493	        try {
   494	                var result;
   495	
   496	                if (fn) {
   497	                        flush_effects();
   498	                        result = fn();
   499	                }
   500	
   501	                while (true) {
   502	                        flush_tasks();
   503	
   504	                        if (queued_root_effects.length === 0) {
   505	                                current_batch?.flush();
   506	
   507	                                // we need to check again, in case we just updated an `$effect.pending()`
   508	                                if (queued_root_effects.length === 0) {
   509	                                        // this would be reset in `flush_effects()` but since we are early returning here,
   510	                                        // we need to reset it here as well in case the first time there's 0 queued root effects
   511	                                        last_scheduled_effect = null;
   512	
   513	                                        return /** @type {T} */ (result);
   514	                                }
   515	                        }
   516	
   517	                        flush_effects();
   518	                }
   519	        } finally {
   520	                is_flushing_sync = was_flushing_sync;
   521	        }
   522	}
   523	
   524	function flush_effects() {
   525	        var was_updating_effect = is_updating_effect;
   526	        is_flushing = true;
   527	
   528	        try {
   529	                var flush_count = 0;
   530	                set_is_updating_effect(true);
   531	
   532	                while (queued_root_effects.length > 0) {
   533	                        var batch = Batch.ensure();
   534	
   535	                        if (flush_count++ > 1000) {
   536	                                if (DEV) {
   537	                                        var updates = new Map();
   538	
   539	                                        for (const source of batch.current.keys()) {
   540	                                                for (const [stack, update] of source.updated ?? []) {
   541	                                                        var entry = updates.get(stack);
   542	
   543	                                                        if (!entry) {
   544	                                                                entry = { error: update.error, count: 0 };
   545	                                                                updates.set(stack, entry);
   546	                                                        }
   547	
   548	                                                        entry.count += update.count;
   549	                                                }
   550	                                        }
   551	
   552	                                        for (const update of updates.values()) {
   553	                                                // eslint-disable-next-line no-console
   554	                                                console.error(update.error);
   555	                                        }
   556	                                }
   557	
   558	                                infinite_loop_guard();
   559	                        }
   560	
   561	                        batch.process(queued_root_effects);
   562	                        old_values.clear();
   563	                }
   564	        } finally {
   565	                is_flushing = false;
   566	                set_is_updating_effect(was_updating_effect);
   567	
   568	                last_scheduled_effect = null;
   569	        }
   570	}
   571	
   572	function infinite_loop_guard() {
   573	        try {
   574	                e.effect_update_depth_exceeded();
   575	        } catch (error) {
   576	                if (DEV) {
   577	                        // stack contains no useful information, replace it
   578	                        define_property(error, 'stack', { value: '' });
   579	                }
   580	
   581	                // Best effort: invoke the boundary nearest the most recent
   582	                // effect and hope that it's relevant to the infinite loop
   583	                invoke_error_boundary(error, last_scheduled_effect);
   584	        }
   585	}
   586	
   587	/**
   588	 * @param {Array<Effect>} effects
   589	 * @returns {void}
   590	 */
   591	function flush_queued_effects(effects) {
   592	        var length = effects.length;
   593	        if (length === 0) return;
   594	
   595	        var i = 0;
   596	
   597	        while (i < length) {
   598	                var effect = effects[i++];
   599	
   600	                if ((effect.f & (DESTROYED | INERT)) === 0 && is_dirty(effect)) {
   601	                        var n = current_batch ? current_batch.current.size : 0;
   602	
   603	                        update_effect(effect);
   604	
   605	                        // Effects with no dependencies or teardown do not get added to the effect tree.
   606	                        // Deferred effects (e.g. `$effect(...)`) _are_ added to the tree because we
   607	                        // don't know if we need to keep them until they are executed. Doing the check
   608	                        // here (rather than in `update_effect`) allows us to skip the work for
   609	                        // immediate effects.
   610	                        if (effect.deps === null && effect.first === null && effect.nodes_start === null) {
   611	                                // if there's no teardown or abort controller we completely unlink
   612	                                // the effect from the graph
   613	                                if (effect.teardown === null && effect.ac === null) {
   614	                                        // remove this effect from the graph
   615	                                        unlink_effect(effect);
   616	                                } else {
   617	                                        // keep the effect in the graph, but free up some memory
   618	                                        effect.fn = null;
   619	                                }
   620	                        }
   621	
   622	                        // if state is written in a user effect, abort and re-schedule, lest we run
   623	                        // effects that should be removed as a result of the state change
   624	                        if (
   625	                                current_batch !== null &&
   626	                                current_batch.current.size > n &&
   627	                                (effect.f & USER_EFFECT) !== 0
   628	                        ) {
   629	                                break;
   630	                        }
   631	                }
   632	        }
   633	
   634	        while (i < length) {
   635	                schedule_effect(effects[i++]);
   636	        }
   637	}
   638	
   639	/**
   640	 * @param {Effect} signal
   641	 * @returns {void}
   642	 */
   643	export function schedule_effect(signal) {
   644	        var effect = (last_scheduled_effect = signal);
   645	
   646	        while (effect.parent !== null) {
   647	                effect = effect.parent;
   648	                var flags = effect.f;
   649	
   650	                // if the effect is being scheduled because a parent (each/await/etc) block
   651	                // updated an internal source, bail out or we'll cause a second flush
   652	                if (is_flushing && effect === active_effect && (flags & BLOCK_EFFECT) !== 0) {
   653	                        return;
   654	                }
   655	
   656	                if ((flags & (ROOT_EFFECT | BRANCH_EFFECT)) !== 0) {
   657	                        if ((flags & CLEAN) === 0) return;
   658	                        effect.f ^= CLEAN;
   659	                }
   660	        }
   661	
   662	        queued_root_effects.push(effect);
   663	}
   664	
   665	export function suspend() {
   666	        var boundary = get_pending_boundary();
   667	        var batch = /** @type {Bat<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. You should retry this tool after you have searched inside the file with `grep -n` in order to find the line numbers of what you are looking for.</NOTE>

   148	 * If it is MAYBE_DIRTY, will set the status to CLEAN
   149	 * @param {Reaction} reaction
   150	 * @returns {boolean}
   151	 */
   152	export function is_dirty(reaction) {
   153	        var flags = reaction.f;
   154	
   155	        if ((flags & DIRTY) !== 0) {
   156	                return true;
   157	        }
   158	
   159	        if ((flags & MAYBE_DIRTY) !== 0) {
   160	                var dependencies = reaction.deps;
   161	                var is_unowned = (flags & UNOWNED) !== 0;
   162	
   163	                if (dependencies !== null) {
   164	                        var i;
   165	                        var dependency;
   166	                        var is_disconnected = (flags & DISCONNECTED) !== 0;
   167	                        var is_unowned_connected = is_unowned && active_effect !== null && !skip_reaction;
   168	                        var length = dependencies.length;
   169	
   170	                        // If we are working with a disconnected or an unowned signal that is now connected (due to an active effect)
   171	                        // then we need to re-connect the reaction to the dependency, unless the effect has already been destroyed
   172	                        // (which can happen if the derived is read by an async derived)
   173	                        if (
   174	                                (is_disconnected || is_unowned_connected) &&
   175	                                (active_effect === null || (active_effect.f & DESTROYED) === 0)
   176	                        ) {
   177	                                var derived = /** @type {Derived} */ (reaction);
   178	                                var parent = derived.parent;
   179	
   180	                                for (i = 0; i < length; i++) {
   181	                                        dependency = dependencies[i];
   182	
   183	                                        // We always re-add all reactions (even duplicates) if the derived was
   184	                                        // previously disconnected, however we don't if it was unowned as we
   185	                                        // de-duplicate dependencies in that case
   186	                                        if (is_disconnected || !dependency?.reactions?.includes(derived)) {
   187	                                                (dependency.reactions ??= []).push(derived);
   188	                                        }
   189	                                }
   190	
   191	                                if (is_disconnected) {
   192	                                        derived.f ^= DISCONNECTED;
   193	                                }
   194	                                // If the unowned derived is now fully connected to the graph again (it's unowned and reconnected, has a parent
   195	                                // and the parent is not unowned), then we can mark it as connected again, removing the need for the unowned
   196	                                // flag
   197	                                if (is_unowned_connected && parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0) {
   198	                                        derived.f ^= UNOWNED;

   223	        validate_effect('$effect.pre');
   224	        if (DEV) {
   225	                define_property(fn, 'name', {
   226	                        value: '$effect.pre'
   227	                });
   228	        }
   229	        return create_effect(RENDER_EFFECT | USER_EFFECT, fn, true);
   230	}
   231	
   232	/** @param {() => void | (() => void)} fn */
   233	export function inspect_effect(fn) {
   234	        return create_effect(INSPECT_EFFECT, fn, true);
   235	}
   236	
   237	/**
   238	 * Internal representation of `$effect.root(...)`
   239	 * @param {() => void | (() => void)} fn
   240	 * @returns {() => void}
   241	 */
   242	export function effect_root(fn) {
   243	        Batch.ensure();
   244	        const effect = create_effect(ROOT_EFFECT, fn, true);
   245	
   246	        return () => {
   247	                destroy_effect(effect);
   248	        };
   249	}

    77	/**
    78	 * `onMount`, like [`$effect`](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/$effect), schedules a function to run as soon as the component has been mounted to the DOM.
    79	 * Unlike `$effect`, the provided function only runs once.
    80	 *
    81	 * It must be called during the component's initialisation (but doesn't need to live _inside_ the component;
    82	 * it can be called from an external module). If a function is returned _synchronously_ from `onMount`,
    83	 * it will be called when the component is unmounted.
    84	 *
    85	 * `onMount` functions do not run during [server-side rendering](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/svelte-server#render).
    86	 *
    87	 * @template T
    88	 * @param {() => NotFunction<T> | Promise<NotFunction<T>> | (() => any)} fn
    89	 * @returns {void}
    90	 */
    91	export function onMount(fn) {
    92	        if (component_context === null) {
    93	                e.lifecycle_outside_component('onMount');
    94	        }
    95	
    96	        if (legacy_mode_flag && component_context.l !== null) {
    97	                init_update_callbacks(component_context).m.push(fn);
    98	        } else {
    99	                user_effect(() => {
   100	                        const cleanup = untrack(fn);
   101	                        if (typeof cleanup === 'function') return /** @type {() => void} */ (cleanup);
   102	                });
   103	        }
   104	}

   111	 *

   115	export function onDestroy(fn) {
   116	        if (component_context === null) {
   117	                e.lifecycle_outside_component('onDestroy');
   118	        }
   119	
   120	        onMount(() => () => untrack(fn));

   130	function create_custom_event(type, detail, { bubbles = false, cancelable = false } = {}) {
   131	        return new CustomEvent(type, { detail, bubbles, cancelable });
   132	}
   133	
   134	/**
   135	 * Creates an event dispatcher that can be used to dispatch [component events](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/legacy-on#Component-events).
   136	 * Event dispatchers are functions that can take two arguments: `name` and `detail`.
   137	 *
   138	 * Component events created with `createEventDispatcher` create a
   139	 * [CustomEvent](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/CustomEvent).
   140	 * These events do not [bubble](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/JavaScript/Building_blocks/Events#Event_bubbling_and_capture).
   141	 * The `detail` argument corresponds to the [CustomEvent.detail](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/CustomEvent/detail)
   142	 * property and can contain any type of data.
   143	 *
   144	 * The event dispatcher can be typed to narrow the allowed event names and the type of the `detail` argument:
   145	 * ```ts
   146	 * const dispatch = createEventDispatcher<{
   147	 *  loaded: null; // does not take a detail argument
   148	 *  change: string; // takes a detail argument of type string, which is required
   149	 *  optional: number | null; // takes an optional detail argument of type number
   150	 * }>();
   151	 * ```
   152	 *
   153	 * @deprecated Use callback props and/or the `$host()` rune instead — see [migration guide](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/v5-migration-guide#Event-changes-Component-events)
   154	 * @template {Record<string, any>} [EventMap = any]
   155	 * @returns {EventDispatcher<EventMap>}
   156	 */
   157	export function createEventDispatcher() {
   158	        const active_component_context = component_context;
   159	        if (active_component_context === null) {
   160	                e.lifecycle_outside_component('createEventDispatcher');
   161	        }
   162	
   163	        return (type, detail, options) => {
   164	                const events = /** @type {Record<string, Function | Function[]>} */ (
   165	                        active_component_context.s.$$events
   166	                )?.[/** @type {any} */ (type)];
   167	
   168	                if (events) {
   169	                        const callbacks = is_array(events) ? events.slice() : [events];
   170	                        // TODO are there situations where events could be dispatched
   171	                        // in a server (non-DOM) environment?

   173	                        for (const fn of callbacks) {
   174	                                fn.call(active_component_context.x, event);
   175	                        }
   176	                        return !event.defaultPrevented;
   177	                }
   178	
   179	                return true;
   180	        };
   181	}

    19	 * @deprecated Use this only as a temporary solution to migrate your imperative component code to Svelte 5.

    35	
    36	/**
    37	 * Takes the component function and returns a Svelte 4 compatible component constructor.
    38	 *
    39	 * @deprecated Use this only as a temporary solution to migrate your imperative component code to Svelte 5.
    40	 *
    41	 * @template {Record<string, any>} Props
    42	 * @template {Record<string, any>} Exports
    43	 * @template {Record<string, any>} Events
    44	 * @template {Record<string, any>} Slots
    45	 *
    46	 * @param {SvelteComponent<Props, Events, Slots> | Component<Props>} component
    47	 * @returns {ComponentType<SvelteComponent<Props, Events, Slots> & Exports>}
    48	 */
    49	export function asClassComponent(component) {
    50	        // @ts-expect-error $$prop_def etc are not actually defined
    51	        return class extends Svelte4Component {
    52	                /** @param {any} options */
    53	                constructor(options) {
    54	                        super({
    55	                                component,
    56	                                ...options
    57	                        });
    58	                }
    59	        };
    60	}
    61	
    62	/**
    63	 * Support using the component as both a class and function during the transition period
    64	 * @typedef  {{new (o: ComponentConstructorOptions): SvelteComponent;(...args: Parameters<Component<Record<string, any>>>): ReturnType<Component<Record<string, any>, Record<string, any>>>;}} LegacyComponentType
    65	 */
    66	
    67	class Svelte4Component {
    68	        /** @type {any} */
    69	        #events;
    70	
    71	        /** @type {Record<string, any>} */
    72	        #instance;
    73	
    74	        /**
    75	         * @param {ComponentConstructorOptions & {
    76	         *  component: any;
    77	         * }} options
    78	         */
    79	        constructor(options) {
    80	                var sources = new Map();
    81	
    82	                /**
    83	                 * @param {string | symbol} key
    84	                 * @param {unknown} value
    85	                 */
    86	                var add_source = (key, value) => {
    87	                        var s = mutable_source(value, false, false);
    88	                        sources.set(key, s);
    89	                        return s;
    90	                };
    91	
    92	                // Replicate coarse-grained props through a proxy that has a version source for
    93	                // each property, which is incremented on updates to the property itself. Do not
    94	                // use our $state proxy because that one has fine-grained reactivity.
    95	                const props = new Proxy(
    96	                        { ...(options.props || {}), $$events: {} },
    97	                        {
    98	                                get(target, prop) {
    99	                                        return get(sources.get(prop) ?? add_source(prop, Reflect.get(target, prop)));
   100	                                },
   101	                                has(target, prop) {
   102	                                        // Necessary to not throw "invalid binding" validation errors on the component side
   103	                                        if (prop === LEGACY_PROPS) return true;
   104	
   105	                                        get(sources.get(prop) ?? add_source(prop, Reflect.get(target, prop)));
   106	                                        return Reflect.has(target, prop);
   107	                                },
   108	                                set(target, prop, value) {
   109	                                        set(sources.get(prop) ?? add_source(prop, value), value);
   110	                                        return Reflect.set(target, prop, value);
   111	                                }
   112	                        }
   113	                );
   114	
   115	                this.#instance = (options.hydrate ? hydrate : mount)(options.component, {
   116	                        target: options.target,
   117	                        anchor: options.anchor,
   118	                        props,
   119	                        context: options.context,
   120	                        intro: options.intro ?? false,
   121	                        recover: options.recover
   122	                });
   123	
   124	                // We don't flushSync for custom element wrappers or if the user doesn't want it,
   125	                // or if we're in async mode since `flushSync()` will fail
   126	                if (!async_mode_flag && (!options?.props?.$$host || options.sync === false)) {
   127	                        flushSync();
   128	                }
   129	
   130	                this.#events = props.$$events;
   131	
   132	                for (const key of Object.keys(this.#instance)) {
   133	                        if (key === '$set' || key === '$destroy' || key === '$on') continue;
   134	                        define_property(this, key, {
   135	                                get() {
   136	                                        return this.#instance[key];
   137	                                },
   138	                                /** @param {any} value */
   139	                                set(value) {
   140	                                        this.#instance[key] = value;
   141	                                },
   142	                                enumerable: true
   143	                        });
   144	                }
   145	
   146	                this.#instance.$set = /** @param {Record<string, any>} next */ (next) => {
   147	                        Object.assign(props, next);
   148	                };
   149	
   150	                this.#instance.$destroy = () => {
   151	                        unmount(this.#instance);
   152	                };
   153	        }
   154	
   155	        /** @param {Record<string, any>} props */
   156	        $set(props) {
   157	                this.#instance.$set(props);
   158	        }
   159	
   160	        /**
   161	         * @param {string} event
   162	         * @param {(...args: any[]) => any} callback
   163	         * @returns {any}
   164	         */
   165	        $on(event, callback) {
   166	                this.#events[event] = this.#events[event] || [];
   167	
   168	                /** @param {any[]} args */
   169	                const cb = (...args) => callback.call(this, ...args);
   170	                this.#events[event].push(cb);
   171	                return () => {
   172	                        this.#events[event] = this.#events[event].filter(/** @param {any} fn */ (fn) => fn !== cb);
   173	                };
   174	        }
   175	
   176	        $destroy() {
   177	                this.#instance.$destroy();
   178	        }
   179	}
   180	
   181	/**
   182	 * Runs the given function once immediately on the server, and works like `$effect.pre` on the client.
   183	 *
   184	 * @deprecated Use this only as a temporary solution to migrate your component code to Svelte 5.
   185	 * @param {() => void | (() => void)} fn
   186	 * @returns {void}
   187	 */
   188	export function run(fn) {
   189	        user_pre_effect(() => {
   190	                fn();
   191	                var effect = /** @type {import('#client').Effect} */ (active_effect);
   192	                // If the effect is immediately made dirty again, mark it as maybe dirty to emulate legacy behaviour
   193	                if ((effect.f & DIRTY) !== 0) {
   194	                        let filename = "a file (we can't know which one)";
   195	                        if (DEV) {
   196	                                // @ts-ignore
   197	                                filename = dev_current_component_function?.[FILENAME] ?? filename;
   198	                        }
   199	                        w.legacy_recursive_reactive_block(filename);
   200	                        set_signal_status(effect, MAYBE_DIRTY);
   201	                }
   202	        });
   203	}
   204	
   205	/**
   206	 * Function to mimic the multiple listeners available in svelte 4
   207	 * @deprecated
   208	 * @param {EventListener[]} handlers
   209	 * @returns {EventListener}
   210	 */
   211	export function handlers(...handlers) {
   212	        return function (event) {
   213	                const { stopImmediatePropagation } = event;
   214	                let stopped = false;
   215	
   216	                event.stopImmediatePropagation = () => {
   217	                        stopped = true;
   218	                        stopImmediatePropagation.call(event);
   219	                };
   220	
   221	                const errors = [];
   222	
   223	                for (const handler of handlers) {
   224	                        try {
   225	                                // @ts-expect-error `this` is not typed
   226	                                handler?.call(this, event);
   227	                        } catch (e) {
   228	                                errors.push(e);
   229	                        }
   230	
   231	                        if (stopped) {
   232	                                break;
   233	                        }
   234	                }
   235	
   236	                for (let error of errors) {
   237	                        queueMicrotask(() => {
   238	                                throw error;
   239	                        });
   240	                }
   241	        };
   242	}
   243	
   244	/**
   245	 * Function to create a `bubble` function that mimic the behavior of `on:click` without handler available in svelte 4.
   246	 * @deprecated Use this only as a temporary solution to migrate your automatically delegated events in Svelte 5.
   247	 */
   248	export function createBubbler() {
   249	        const active_component_context = component_context;
   250	        if (active_component_context === null) {
   251	                e.lifecycle_outside_component('createBubbler');
   252	        }
   253	
   254	        return (/**@type {string}*/ type) => (/**@type {Event}*/ event) => {
   255	                const events = /** @type {Record<string, Function | Function[]>} */ (
   256	                        active_component_context.s.$$events
   257	                )?.[/** @type {any} */ (type)];
   258	
   259	                if (events) {
   260	                        const callbacks = is_array(events) ? events.slice() : [events];
   261	                        for (const fn of callbacks) {
   262	                                fn.call(active_component_context.x, event);
   263	                        }
   264	                        return !event.defaultPrevented;
   265	                }
   266	                return true;
   267	        };
   268	}
   269	
   270	export {
   271	        once,
   272	        preventDefault,
   273	        self,
   274	        stopImmediatePropagation,
   275	        stopPropagation,
   276	        trusted,
   277	        passive,
   278	        nonpassive
   279	} from '../internal/client/dom/legacy/event-modifiers.js';
